1. Introduction
1.1 Purpose
हा Document PreOne च्या Physical Database Schema चा authoritative reference आहे. DDD v1.0 ने business domain ला software model मध्ये translate केले; या document त्या software model ची physical implementation detail देतो — कोणते tables, कोणते columns, कोणते indexes, कोणते constraints, आणि कोणते relationships. PRD चे Functional Requirements आणि BRC चे Business Rules या schema द्वारे enforce होतात.
याच Document वरून पुढील गोष्टी तयार होतील: Prisma Schema (TypeScript ORM definitions), Migrations (version-controlled DDL), Backend Repositories (data access layer), Data Warehouse ETL (CDC pipelines), Analytics Cubes (for BI dashboards), आणि AI Training Data Extracts (for ML model training). हा document हा database layer चा single source of truth आहे.
Document चा primary audience हा database engineers, backend developers, data engineers, आणि architects आहे. Business analysts आणि product managers यांनी domain chapters च्या overview आणि KPI sections वाचून business meaning capture करावा; column-level details हे engineering reference आहेत.
1.2 Scope
हा document फक्त database physical layer cover करतो. खालील गोष्टी scope बाहेर आहेत:
•  Application Layer Design नाही — Service classes, Use Cases, आणि Controllers ची detail DDD v1.0 मध्ये आहे.
•  API Contract नाही — REST endpoints, request/response schemas API Contract Catalog v1.0 मध्ये separate आहेत.
•  UI/UX Specs नाही — Screen designs, interaction flows UI/UX spec मध्ये आहेत.
•  Infrastructure Topology नाही — Kubernetes manifests, Terraform modules, observability stack separate run-book मध्ये.
•  Application Caching Strategy नाही — Redis cache key conventions, invalidation rules वेगळ्या caching strategy doc मध्ये.
Scope फक्त हा आहे: PostgreSQL 16 schema definition, naming conventions, data type standards, indexing strategy, constraints, multi-tenancy implementation, audit/soft-delete patterns, security & DPDP compliance, आणि per-domain data dictionary.
1.3 Audience
हा document खालील audiences साठी लिखित आहे:
•  Database Engineers: DDL generation, migration authoring, performance tuning, indexing decisions साठी primary reference.
•  Backend Engineers: Prisma schema generation, repository implementation, query optimization साठी.
•  Data Engineers: ETL pipeline design, CDC source identification, warehouse schema design साठी.
•  Architects: Multi-tenancy decisions, partitioning strategy, read replica topology साठी.
•  QA Engineers: Test data setup, edge case identification (FK ON DELETE behavior, soft-delete recovery) साठी.
•  Compliance Officers: PII column inventory, retention rules, audit trail coverage साठी.
•  AI Code Assistants: Each section structured as prompt-able block; AI tools (Cursor, Copilot) च्या context मध्ये दिल्यावर Prisma schema, migration SQL, आणि repository code accurate generate होते.
1.4 Document Conventions
•  Table names: snake_case, plural where natural (students, audit_log).
•  Column names: snake_case, no abbreviations (created_at not crt_at).
•  Foreign keys: <entity>_id suffix (school_id, branch_id, student_id).
•  Indexes: <table>_<columns>_idx suffix; unique uses _uidx; partial adds _p.
•  Constraints: <table>_<purpose>_ck (check), _fk (foreign), _uq (unique).
•  Enums: PascalCase singular type name (AttendanceStatus); values UPPER_SNAKE_CASE.
•  Primary keys: UUID v7 (time-sortable) — id column.
•  Timestamps: timestamptz (with timezone) for all date/time columns; never plain timestamp.
•  Money: numeric(12,2) or integer cents — never float.
•  Soft delete: deleted_at timestamptz NULL; partial index WHERE deleted_at IS NULL.
•  Bilingual content: Marathi/Hindi business context + English technical terms preserved as user provided.

2. Database Architecture Overview
PreOne हा PostgreSQL 16 वर build आहे. PostgreSQL ची choice खालील reasons ने आहे: ACID compliance, native UUID support, jsonb with GIN indexing, native enum types, row-level security (RLS) for multi-tenancy, partial + expression indexes, point-in-time recovery (PITR), logical replication for read replicas, आणि strong ecosystem (Prisma, pgAdmin, psql, pgvector for AI). PostgreSQL 16 च्या UUID v7 support ने time-sortable primary keys मिळतात जे multi-region writes सह सहज handle करतात.
2.1 Topology
Production topology मध्ये प्रमुख components आहेत: Primary instance (rw), 2 Read replicas (ro — 1 sync, 1 async), PgBouncer connection pooler, WAL archive for PITR, S3 for backups, cross-region replica (DR).
                                                  +-------------------+
                                                  |  Cross-Region DR  |
                                                  |  (async replica)  |
                                                  +---------+---------+
                                                            |
                                                            | WAL stream
                                                            |
  +---------+      +-----------+      +-----------+      +--v----------------+
  |  App    +----->+ PgBouncer +----->+  Primary  +----->+  WAL Archive (S3) |
  | Servers |      |  (pool)   |      |  (rw)     |      |  PITR source      |
  +---------+      +-----+-----+      +-----+-----+      +-------------------+
                         |                  |
                         |                  | logical replication
                         |                  v
                         |            +-----+-----+    +-----------+
                         +----------->+  Replica  |    |  Replica  |
                           read-only  |  (sync)   |    |  (async)  |
                                      +-----------+    +-----------+
                                       analytics       reporting
2.2 Multi-Tenancy Model
PreOne हा shared-schema multi-tenant model वापरतो — सर्व tenants एकच database + schema share करतात, प्रत्येक row मध्ये school_id column tenant discriminator म्हणून काम करतो. हा model chosen कारण tenant count 10,000+ असेल आणि per-tenant database maintain करणे operationally expensive होईल.
Alternative options considered: schema-per-tenant (rejected — 10k+ schemas degrade catalog performance), database-per-tenant (rejected — operationally unmanageable at scale). Shared schema with RLS हा sweet spot आहे: query performance good, backup/restore simple, migration uniform.
Row-Level Security (RLS) policies enforce tenant isolation at database level. Application connections set school_id via session variable (SET app.school_id = ?); RLS policies automatically filter rows. Cross-tenant access requires platform_admin role + explicit bypass.
2.3 Connection Pooling
PgBouncer transaction-mode pooling वापरतो — 10,000+ concurrent application connections ला ~100 database connections शी multiplex करतो. Pool size per-tenant cap configured केला आहे (max 10 concurrent transactions per tenant) ज्यामुळे noisy-neighbor problem prevent होतो.
2.4 Backup + DR
Backup strategy: PITR via WAL archiving (5-minute RPO), daily logical backup (pg_dump) per tenant for granular restore, weekly full cluster snapshot, monthly restore drill. RTO 30 minutes for single-tenant restore, 2 hours for full cluster restore. Cross-region DR replica maintains async replication; failover run-book documented separately.
2.5 RPO / RTO Targets
Scenario
RPO
RTO
Strategy
Single-row accidental delete
0 (PITR)
15 min
Time travel query via PITR WAL replay
Single-tenant data corruption
5 min
30 min
Logical restore from daily backup
Schema migration failure
0 (snapshot)
20 min
Snapshot restore + rollback migration
Primary failure
0 (sync replica)
5 min
Promote sync replica to primary
Region failure
30 sec (async)
2 hours
Promote cross-region DR replica
Complete cluster loss
5 min
4 hours
Restore from S3 WAL + snapshots
3. Naming Conventions & Standards
Naming conventions हे database maintainability चे foundation आहेत. PreOne मध्ये खालील standards enforce केले जातात — PR review मध्ये convention violations block होतात आणि automated linter (sqlfluff + custom rules) CI pipeline मध्ये run होतो.
3.1 Naming Standards Reference
Element
Convention
Rationale
Tables
snake_case, plural where natural (e.g., students, audit_log)
Plural reads better in JOINs and avoids keyword clashes
Columns
snake_case, no abbreviations (created_at not crt_at)
Long names acceptable — PostgreSQL column names are cheap
Primary Keys
id, type uuid, default uuid_generate_v7()
UUID v7 enables time-sortable keys + multi-region writes
Foreign Keys
<entity>_id, e.g., school_id, branch_id, student_id
Suffix _id is mandatory; composite FKs use _oid pair
Indexes
<table>_<columns>_idx, e.g., students_branch_id_idx
_idx suffix; unique uses _uidx; partial adds _p suffix
Constraints
<table>_<purpose>_ck for check, _fk for foreign, _uq for unique
Explicit naming aids migration review + ROLLBACK
Enums
PascalCase singular (AttendanceStatus, InvoiceStatus)
Stored as native PG enum; values UPPER_SNAKE_CASE
Timestamps
timestamptz for all date/time columns
Never use timestamp without tz — multi-region breaks it
Money
numeric(12,2) — never float, never integer paise
12 digits + 2 decimals covers INR/USD with safety margin
Boolean
boolean with default false; column name starts with is_ or has_
Avoids ambiguity with status enums
JSON
jsonb for structured config, jsonb GIN index when queried
Never use json (text-only) — loses query optimization
Soft Delete
deleted_at timestamptz NULL; partial index WHERE deleted_at IS NULL
Restores via UPDATE; permanent delete via admin tool only
3.2 Examples
Concrete examples खालीलप्रमाणे:
-- Tables
CREATE TABLE students (...);
CREATE TABLE audit_log (...);
 
-- Columns
school_id      UUID NOT NULL,
created_at     timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
student_code   varchar(20),
 
-- Indexes
CREATE INDEX students_branch_id_idx        ON students(branch_id);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX students_student_code_uidx ON students(student_code);
CREATE INDEX students_active_idx           ON students(branch_id)
  WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
 
-- Constraints
CONSTRAINT students_status_ck CHECK (status IN ('ACTIVE','INACTIVE','GRADUATED')),
CONSTRAINT students_school_fk FOREIGN KEY (school_id) REFERENCES schools(id)
  ON DELETE RESTRICT
 
-- Enums
CREATE TYPE AttendanceStatus AS ENUM ('PRESENT','ABSENT','LATE','HALF_DAY','LEAVE');
4. Data Type Standards
Data type choice हे storage efficiency, query performance, आणि correctness लाखो rows मध्ये affect करतो. PreOne मध्ये खालील type standards enforce केले जातात — दर type चे specific use case + size characteristics document केले आहेत.
4.1 Type Reference
Type
Use Case
Notes
UUID
id columns, FKs, public tokens
uuid_generate_v7() default; 16 bytes; time-sortable
timestamptz
all timestamps
8 bytes; range 4713 BC–294276 AD
date
calendar dates without time
4 bytes; use for birth_date, invoice_date
numeric(12,2)
money amounts
variable; 12 digits total, 2 after decimal
numeric(5,2)
percentages, rates
0.00 to 999.99 range
integer
counts, quantities
4 bytes; sufficient for student counts
bigint
audit IDs, sequence counters
8 bytes; required for >2B row tables
text
long-form, variable strings
No length limit; use over varchar unless index constraint
varchar(n)
codes, identifiers with fixed max
Use only when business rule mandates max length
citext
emails, usernames (case-insensitive)
Requires citext extension; auto lower-cases comparisons
boolean
flags, toggles
1 byte; always default false unless true
jsonb
structured config, flexible payloads
Binary JSON; GIN-indexable; no order preservation
bytea
encrypted blobs, signatures
Avoid for large files — use object storage + URL
enum
closed status sets
Native PG enum; cannot delete values — plan carefully
int4range
academic year ranges, date ranges
Enables exclusion constraints for overlap prevention
4.2 Money Handling
Money columns नेहमी integer cents मध्ये store होतात (e.g., amount_cents) किंवा numeric(12,2) मध्ये. Float types (real, double precision) हे money साठी FORBIDDEN आहेत कारण rounding errors compound होतात. Integer cents preferred कारण integer arithmetic float च्या comparison अधिक fast आणि exact आहे. Display time ला divide by 100 करून decimal show करावे.
4.3 Timestamps
सर्व timestamp columns ने timestamptz (timestamp with timezone) वापरावे. PostgreSQL internally UTC मध्ये store करतो पण display timezone session setting नुसार adjust होतो. Multi-region deployment मध्ये timestamp without tz columns ambiguous होतात आणि subtle bugs introduce करतात. Created_at आणि updated_at साठी DEFAULT now() वापरा; updated_at साठी trigger-based auto-update.
4.4 JSON vs JSONB
jsonb हा default choice आहे — binary storage, GIN-indexable, faster query. json (text-storage) हे केवळ order-preserving need असल्यास वापरा (जे दुर्मिळ आहे). PreOne मध्ये config columns, flexible metadata, आणि arrays सर्व jsonb मध्ये store होतात.
4.5 Enums vs Lookup Tables
Closed status sets (≤10 values, जे कधीच change होणार नाहीत) साठी native PG enum वापरा (AttendanceStatus, InvoiceStatus). Open or evolving sets साठी lookup table वापरा (inventory_categories, fee_heads). Enum values delete होऊ शकत नाहीत — त्यामुळे जर कधी value remove करायचा असेल तर lookup table better आहे.
5. Multi-Tenancy Strategy
Multi-tenancy हे PreOne च्या architecture चा core decision आहे. Shared-schema model ने tenant isolation + operational simplicity चा balance साधला आहे. या section मध्ये implementation details + operational procedures document आहेत.
5.1 Tenant Discriminator
प्रत्येक tenant-scoped table मध्ये school_id UUID NOT NULL column असतो जो schools(id) ला references करतो. हा column प्रत्येक composite index चा prefix आहे ज्यामुळे tenant-scanned queries efficient होतात. RLS policies school_id ला session variable app.school_id शी compare करतात.
-- Example RLS policy
ALTER TABLE students ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
 
CREATE POLICY students_tenant_isolation ON students
  USING (school_id = current_setting('app.school_id')::uuid);
 
-- Application sets school_id on connection checkout:
-- SET app.school_id = '5f3e2a1b-...';
5.2 Tenant-Scoped Connections
PgBouncer pooler ला tenant-aware config केले आहे. Application layer connection acquire करताना SET app.school_id = ? query run करते; connection release करताना RESET app.school_id run करते. हे discipline न राखल्यास cross-tenant data leak होऊ शकतो — transaction-level isolation देखील enable केले आहे.
5.3 Cross-Tenant Admin Endpoints
Platform admin operations (billing aggregation, storage metering, platform integrations) ला cross-tenant access आवश्यक आहे. अशा endpoints साठी dedicated platform_admin database role आहे ज्याला BYPASSRLS privilege आहे. हे connections वेगळ्या pool मधून serve होतात; audit log मध्ये प्रत्येक query record होते.
5.4 Tenant Isolation Audit
Quarterly audit job प्रत्येक table मधील school_id distribution check करतो — कोणत्याही row मध्ये school_id NULL असल्यास alert raise होतो (except for global tables जसे global_configuration, permissions). ही audit DPDP compliance चा part आहे — कोणत्याही tenant चा data दुसऱ्या ला leak नसावा.
6. Indexing Strategy
Indexing हे database performance चा single most important factor आहे. PreOne मध्ये indexing strategy documented, deliberate, आणि measured आहे. प्रत्येक index चा specific query pattern serve करतो — नको ते indexes write performance degrade करतात आणि storage waste होतो.
6.1 Index Type Reference
Type
When to Use
Example
btree
Equality + range queries (default)
student_id = ?, created_at BETWEEN ? AND ?
btree_unique
Natural key uniqueness enforcement
student_code, invoice_number
gin
jsonb containment queries
config @> '{"key":"value"}'
gist
Geometric + full-text search + range overlaps
tsrange overlap exclusion
brin
Time-series tables (append-only, naturally ordered)
audit_log.occurred_at
partial
Subset of rows often queried
WHERE deleted_at IS NULL, WHERE is_active = true
expression
Function-based lookup
lower(email)
composite
Multiple columns often queried together
(school_id, branch_id, status)
covering (INCLUDE)
Additional columns to avoid heap fetch
Index-only scans for hot paths
6.2 Common Index Patterns in PreOne
•  Foreign key columns always indexed — PostgreSQL does NOT auto-index FKs.
•  Partial index WHERE deleted_at IS NULL on soft-delete tables — active rows only.
•  Partial index WHERE is_active = true on status-flag tables — active records only.
•  Composite index (school_id, branch_id, ...) — tenant + scope pruning.
•  BRIN on time-series tables (audit_log, sms_log, trip_log) — 90% smaller than btree.
•  GIN on jsonb config columns — @> containment queries.
•  Unique indexes on natural keys (student_code, invoice_number, phone) — enforce business uniqueness.
6.3 Index Maintenance
Index bloat monitoring weekly run होतो — pages_reclaimed आणि fragmentation ratio track होतो. REINDEX CONCURRENTLY scheduled monthly for high-write tables (audit_log, sms_log, attendances). Auto-vacuum tuned per-table — high-write tables get aggressive autovacuum settings; low-write tables default.
7. Constraints & Validation Strategy
Constraints हे data integrity चे last line of defense आहेत. Application-layer validation user-friendly error messages देते पण database constraints enforce guarantee देतात. PreOne मध्ये defense-in-depth approach आहे — both layers active.
7.1 Constraint Types Used
Constraint
Purpose
Example
PRIMARY KEY
Row uniqueness
id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v7()
FOREIGN KEY
Referential integrity
school_id REFERENCES schools(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT
UNIQUE
Business uniqueness
UNIQUE(school_id, student_code)
CHECK
Domain constraints
CHECK (status IN ('ACTIVE','INACTIVE'))
NOT NULL
Mandatory fields
school_id UUID NOT NULL
EXCLUSION
Range overlaps prevention
EXCLUDE USING gist (tsrange WITH &&)
DEFAULT
Default values
DEFAULT now(), DEFAULT false, DEFAULT 0
7.2 FK ON DELETE Behaviors
FK ON DELETE behavior हा data integrity चा critical decision आहे. PreOne मध्ये खालील rules enforce होतात:
•  RESTRICT — parent table deletion blocked (default for school, branch, student, user).
•  CASCADE — child rows auto-deleted (for junction tables, e.g., role_permission, user_role).
•  SET NULL — child FK set to NULL (for soft references, e.g., approved_by, created_by).
•  Hard deletes दुर्मिळ — soft delete (deleted_at) preferred. RESTRICT केवळ schema-migration safety साठी.
7.3 CHECK Constraints for Enum Validation
Native PG enums type-safe आहेत पण migration burden जास्त (value add करण्यास migrate करावे लागते). PreOne मध्ये hybrid approach: critical enums (AttendanceStatus, InvoiceStatus) native enum; evolving enums varchar + CHECK constraint. CHECK constraint faster migrate करता येतो.
7.4 Exclusion Constraints
Time-overlapping entities (room bookings, staff shifts, classroom assignments) साठी exclusion constraints enforce केले आहेत. 例: room_booking table मध्ये EXCLUDE USING gist (room_id WITH =, tsrange(start_at, end_at) WITH &&) — एकाच room मध्ये overlapping booking prevent होते.
8. Audit, Soft-Delete & Versioning
Data integrity + forensic audit + DPDP compliance यांसाठी audit + soft-delete + versioning patterns standardize केले आहेत. या section मध्ये implementation patterns document आहेत.
8.1 Soft Delete Pattern
Hard deletes दुर्मिळ आहेत — प्रत्येक business table मध्ये deleted_at timestamptz NULL column आहे. Row 'delete' म्हणजे UPDATE ... SET deleted_at = now(). Restore म्हणजे UPDATE ... SET deleted_at = NULL. Permanent delete हा admin tool द्वारे manual — दर permanent delete audit_log मध्ये record होतो.
-- Soft delete trigger (simplified)
CREATE TRIGGER soft_delete_before_delete
  BEFORE DELETE ON students
  FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION soft_delete_handler();
 
CREATE FUNCTION soft_delete_handler() RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
  UPDATE students SET deleted_at = now() WHERE id = OLD.id;
  RETURN NULL;  -- suppress actual DELETE
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;
8.2 Audit Log Pattern
audit_log table हा immutable forensics record आहे — कधीच UPDATE/DELETE होत नाही. प्रत्येक CREATE/UPDATE/DELETE म्हणजे INSERT into audit_log. Trigger-based logging हा default; application-layer logging केवळ cross-service operations साठी. audit_log monthly partitioned (1M+ rows/day at scale) — BRIN index on occurred_at.
Audit log columns: user_id (actor), action (CREATE/UPDATE/DELETE/LOGIN/...), module, entity, entity_id, old_values (jsonb), new_values (jsonb), ip_address, user_agent, request_id (distributed tracing), occurred_at.
8.3 Optimistic Concurrency
Critical entities (Student, Invoice, Payment, Application) मध्ये version integer column आहे जो प्रत्येक UPDATE ला increment होतो. Application UPDATE ... SET version = version + 1 WHERE id = ? AND version = ? execute करते; जर 0 rows affected तर concurrent modification detect होते आणि user ला retry prompt केले जाते. हे pattern lost-update anomalies prevent करते.
8.4 History Tables
Specific high-value entities (Student, Invoice, FeePlan, Application) साठी dedicated history tables आहेत — student_history, invoice_history, etc. ह्या tables append-only आहेत आणि प्रत्येक significant lifecycle event snapshot store करतात (admission, promotion, graduation, transfer for students; issue, payment, refund, write-off for invoices). History tables analytical queries साठी optimize केले आहेत.
9. Security & DPDP Compliance Mapping
DPDP (Digital Personal Data Protection) Act 2023 हा India चा primary data protection law आहे. PreOne हा India-based preschool chain साठी आहे आणि DPDP compliance mandatory आहे. या section मध्ये database-level DPDP compliance measures document आहेत.
9.1 PII Classification
Classification
Examples
Handling
Public
School name, branch address, phone (general)
No encryption; index freely
Internal
Student attendance, classroom assignment, academic progress
Tenant-isolated; RLS enforced
Confidential
Parent email, parent phone, staff salary, fee invoices
Encrypted at rest (pgcrypto); masked in non-prod
Restricted
Aadhaar, PAN, bank account, medical records, biometric
Field-level encryption (pgcrypto); access audit; explicit consent per DPDP §11
9.2 Encryption at Rest
Confidential + Restricted columns pgcrypto extension ने encrypted store होतात — column-level encryption. Example: aadhaar_number stored as bytea (pgcrypto symmetric), masked display column aadhaar_number_masked (XXXX-XXXX-XXXX format) for UI. Database-level TDE (Transparent Data Encryption) additional layer — disk-level encryption via LUKS for EBS volumes.
-- Example: Aadhaar encryption
ALTER TABLE students ADD COLUMN aadhaar_encrypted bytea;
ALTER TABLE students ADD COLUMN aadhaar_number varchar(12);
  -- aadhaar_number stores masked: 'XXXX-XXXX-1234'
 
-- On write:
UPDATE students SET
  aadhaar_encrypted = pgp_sym_encrypt('1234-5678-9012', current_setting('app.encryption_key')),

  aadhaar_number = 'XXXX-XXXX-9012'
WHERE id = ?;
9.3 DPDP Section Mapping
DPDP Section
Requirement
Database Implementation
§4 (Consent)
Consent before data collection
Consent table with timestamp + IP + version of consent text
§8 (Purpose Limitation)
Data used only for stated purpose
Data classification + access control per purpose
§11 (Right to Access)
Data subject access request
DSAR endpoint aggregating student + guardian + attendance + finance records
§12 (Right to Correction)
Correction + completion
Correction request table with approval workflow
§13 (Right to Erasure)
Right to be forgotten
Archive + minimize workflow (Section 8 pattern)
§17 (Data Retention)
Retain only as long as necessary
Retention rules per data category; auto-archive after 7 years
§21 (Grievance Redressal)
Grievance officer + response time
grievance_ticket table + SLA enforcement
§33 (Breach Notification)
Breach notification to authority + affected
Security incident table + 72-hour notification workflow
9.4 Data Minimization
Inactive student records 7 years after exit archive होतात — यानंतर PII columns scrubbed होतात (data_minimized = true) आणि केवळ aggregate analytics साठी anonymized record retain होतो. Archive table DPDP §17 चे implementation आहे.
9.5 Access Audit
Confidential + Restricted columns access हा audit log मध्ये special action 'ACCESS' ने record होतो. Quarterly access review compliance officer द्वारे conduct होतो — unexpected access patterns investigate होतात.
10. Domain: Platform Management (SaaS)
हा domain PreOne चा multi-tenant control plane आहे. प्रत्येक school एक tenant आहे; या domain मध्ये subscription billing, storage metering, feature usage tracking, API key management, automated backups, आणि third-party integration registry येतात. Cross-tenant admin endpoints वेगळ्या platform_admin database role ने access होतात.
10.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Monthly Recurring Revenue (MRR)
Sum of active subscription amounts per month
Storage utilization
Per-tenant photos + documents + backups vs plan limit
API call quota
Per-tenant daily API call count vs plan limit
Backup success rate
% of backups in COMPLETED state (target 100%)
Integration health
% of integrations in CONNECTED state (target 99%)
10.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 8 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:

Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.

11. Domain: Core (Auth & Org)
हा domain PreOne चा identity + organization backbone आहे. Schools, branches, users, roles, permissions, sessions — सर्व cross-cutting identity concerns येथे आहेत. RBAC matrix role + permission + role_permission मधून compute होतो; दर session scope मध्ये cached होतो.
11.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Login success rate
≥99% over rolling 24h
Session creation latency
P99 <200ms
Permission check latency
P99 <10ms (in-memory cache)
Account lockout rate
<0.5% of logins (security threshold)
11.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 12 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:
Table
Prisma Model
Aggregate
Purpose
school
School
Tenant
Multi-tenant anchor entity. One school = one tenant. All tenant-scoped tables reference this via school_id.
branch
Branch
Tenant
Physical preschool location under a school (tenant). A school may have multiple branches; each branch has its own classrooms, staff, and students.
user
User
Identity
Application user — staff, parent, or system. Linked via user_role to one or more roles. Authentication via password hash or OTP.
role
Role
Identity
Named permission bundle (Center Head, Teacher, Parent, Accountant). Roles are tenant-scoped; super_admin role is platform-wide.
permission
Permission
Identity
Atomic capability string (e.g., 'fees.refund.execute'). Permissions are platform-wide dictionary; roles attach via role_permission.
role_permission
RolePermission
Identity
Junction table linking roles to permissions. RBAC matrix computed from this + user_role.
user_role
UserRole
Identity
User ↔ role assignment; optionally scoped to a branch or classroom.
session
Session
Identity
Active user session. Used for audit trail and force-logout. JWT is stateless but session table allows revocation.
refresh_token
RefreshToken
Identity
Long-lived refresh token for JWT rotation. Hashed at rest; rotation invalidates previous.
otp_challenge
OtpChallenge
Identity
OTP issued for login / phone verification / passwordless flow. Hashed; rate-limited.
audit_log
AuditLog
PlatformConfig
Immutable forensics record of who-did-what-when. Append-only; never UPDATE/DELETE. Partitioned monthly.
feature_flag
FeatureFlag
PlatformConfig
Tenant-scoped feature flag for progressive rollout. Evaluated at request time and cached.
11.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Core (Auth & Org) (12 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ school                               → Prisma: School
│    Multi-tenant anchor entity. One school = one tenant. All ...
│    Key cols: email(citext), gst_number(varchar(15)), pan_number(varchar(10))
│
│  ◆ branch                               → Prisma: Branch
│    Physical preschool location under a school (tenant). A sc...
│    Key cols: code(varchar(8))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT
│
│  ◆ user                                 → Prisma: User
│    Application user — staff, parent, or system. Linked via u...
│    Key cols: email(citext), phone(varchar(16))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT
│
│  ◆ role                                 → Prisma: Role
│    Named permission bundle (Center Head, Teacher, Parent, Ac...
│    Key cols: code(varchar(32))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ permission                           → Prisma: Permission
│    Atomic capability string (e.g., 'fees.refund.execute'). P...
│    Key cols: code(varchar(80))
│
│  ◆ role_permission                      → Prisma: RolePermission
│    Junction table linking roles to permissions. RBAC matrix ...
│    Key cols: role_id(UUID), permission_id(UUID), granted_by(UUID)
│    FKs: role_id → roles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; permission_id → permissions(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ user_role                            → Prisma: UserRole
│    User ↔ role assignment; optionally scoped to a branch or ...
│    Key cols: user_id(UUID), role_id(UUID), branch_id(UUID), classroom_id(UUID), assigned_by(UUID)
│    FKs: user_id → users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; role_id → roles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ session                              → Prisma: Session
│    Active user session. Used for audit trail and force-logou...
│    Key cols: user_id(UUID), token_jti(varchar(64))
│    FKs: user_id → users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ refresh_token                        → Prisma: RefreshToken
│    Long-lived refresh token for JWT rotation. Hashed at rest...
│    Key cols: user_id(UUID), token_hash(varchar(128))
│    FKs: user_id → users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ otp_challenge                        → Prisma: OtpChallenge
│    OTP issued for login / phone verification / passwordless ...
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ... and 2 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└─────────────────────────────────┘
11.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.

12. Domain: Marketing & CRM
हा domain lead capture से ते conversion पर्यंतचा पूर्ण funnel आहे. Marketing campaigns → leads → enquiries → counselling sessions → application hand-off. Attribution model lead_source शी link होतो; lead_score hot/warm/cold classification automated आहे.
12.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Lead-to-enquiry conversion
≥70% within 7 days
Cost per lead (CPL)
Tracked per campaign channel
Counsellor response time
Median <60 min during business hours
Referral conversion rate
≥35% (highest quality source)
12.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 14 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:
Table
Prisma Model
Aggregate
Purpose
marketing_campaign
MarketingCampaign
Campaign
Marketing campaign record — channel, budget, attribution window.
lead_source
LeadSource
Campaign
Lead source dictionary (walk-in, referral, online ad). Stable reference for attribution.
lead
Lead
Lead
Pre-admission prospect captured from campaigns, walk-ins, referrals. Converts to enquiry after qualification.
lead_activity
LeadActivity
Lead
Timeline of every interaction with a lead — call, WhatsApp, email, visit, demo.
enquiry
Enquiry
Lead
Qualified lead with explicit intent — preferred program + branch + timeframe. Becomes application when documents submitted.
follow_up
FollowUp
Lead
Scheduled follow-up task. Distinct from lead_activity (which records completed actions).
referral
Referral
Lead
Referral record — existing parent refers new lead. Eligibility + reward tracked.
referral_reward
ReferralReward
Lead
Issued referral rewards log. Drives finance reconciliation for fee discounts.
whatsapp_opt_in
WhatsAppOptIn
Lead
Parent consent for WhatsApp marketing messages. Required by DPDP §11.
email_subscription
EmailSubscription
Lead
Parent consent for marketing emails. Unsubscribe tracking per CAN-SPAM/DPDP.
lead_score
LeadScore
Lead
Computed lead score breakdown. Refreshed nightly by job.
lead_conversion
LeadConversion
Lead
Conversion event log — when lead becomes enquiry, enquiry becomes application, application becomes admission.
lead_assignment
LeadAssignment
Lead
Lead-to-counsellor assignment history. Supports round-robin + manual overrides + workload balancing.
marketing_channel
MarketingChannel
Campaign
Channel configuration — API keys, templates, rate limits per channel.
12.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Marketing & CRM (14 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ marketing_campaign                   → Prisma: MarketingCampaign
│    Marketing campaign record — channel, budget, attribution ...
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ lead_source                          → Prisma: LeadSource
│    Lead source dictionary (walk-in, referral, online ad). St...
│    Key cols: name(varchar(64))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ lead                                 → Prisma: Lead
│    Pre-admission prospect captured from campaigns, walk-ins,...
│    Key cols: preferred_branch_id(UUID), source_id(UUID), campaign_id(UUID), referral_lead_id(UUID), ...
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; assigned_to → users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; source_id → lead_sources(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT
│
│  ◆ lead_activity                        → Prisma: LeadActivity
│    Timeline of every interaction with a lead — call, WhatsAp...
│    Key cols: lead_id(UUID), actor_id(UUID)
│    FKs: lead_id → leads(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; actor_id → users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ enquiry                              → Prisma: Enquiry
│    Qualified lead with explicit intent — preferred program +...
│    Key cols: lead_id(UUID), branch_id(UUID)
│    FKs: lead_id → leads(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ follow_up                            → Prisma: FollowUp
│    Scheduled follow-up task. Distinct from lead_activity (wh...
│    Key cols: lead_id(UUID), enquiry_id(UUID), assigned_to(UUID)
│    FKs: lead_id → leads(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; assigned_to → users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ referral                             → Prisma: Referral
│    Referral record — existing parent refers new lead. Eligib...
│    Key cols: referrer_parent_id(UUID), referred_lead_id(UUID), referral_code(varchar(16))
│    FKs: referred_lead_id → leads(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; referrer_parent_id → parents(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ referral_reward                      → Prisma: ReferralReward
│    Issued referral rewards log. Drives finance reconciliatio...
│    Key cols: referral_id(UUID), invoice_credit_id(UUID)
│    FKs: referral_id → referrals(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ whatsapp_opt_in                      → Prisma: WhatsAppOptIn
│    Parent consent for WhatsApp marketing messages. Required ...
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ email_subscription                   → Prisma: EmailSubscription
│    Parent consent for marketing emails. Unsubscribe tracking...
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ... and 4 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└───────────────────────────────┘
12.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.

13. Domain: Admission
हा domain lead → enquiry → application → approval → admission pipeline चा formalization आहे. Age verification per program, document checklist, fee plan quote, आणि multi-level approval matrix येथे आहे. BRC च्या Eligibility + Approval rules या domain मध्ये enforce होतात.
13.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Application-to-approval time
Median ≤7 days
Document verification SLA
≤48 hours
Approval matrix compliance
100% (no bypass)
Waitlist conversion rate
≥40%
13.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 15 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:
Table
Prisma Model

खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.

│    Document uploaded against an application — birth cert, ph...

│    Per-program mandatory document checklist. Drives verifica...

│    Counselling/interaction session with parent + child. Sche...

│    Final admission record created after all approvals. Trigg...

│  ◆ age_verification                     → Prisma: AgeVerification
│    Age eligibility verification per program (BRC R-ELG-001)....
│    Key cols: application_id(UUID), verified_by(UUID)
│    FKs: application_id → applications(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE

13.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
13.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)

14. Domain: Student Lifecycle
हा domain PreOne चा core entity domain आहे. Student master record, parent/guardian records, medical history, classroom assignment, promotion, graduation, transfer, आणि archival — सर्व lifecycle stages येथून manage होतात. DPDP §17 नुसार inactive student records 7 वर्षांनी archive होतात.
14.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Single source of truth
0 duplicate students across branches
Promotion completion time
≤24 hours for entire branch at year-end
Medical record completeness
≥95% students with allergy + immunization
Archive compliance
100% archived after 7 years (DPDP §17)
14.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 22 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:
Table
Prisma Model
Aggregate
Purpose

14.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Student Lifecycle (22 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ student                              → Prisma: Student
│    Master student record. Created at admission; carries iden...
│    Key cols: student_code(varchar(20)), admission_id(UUID), current_branch_id(UUID), current_classro...
│    FKs: admission_id → admissions(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; current_branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; current_classroom_id → classrooms(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; +1 more

│    Extended profile — demographics, custody, address. Separa...

│
│  ◆ guardian                             → Prisma: Guardian
│    Parent/guardian master record. One guardian may be linked...
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│

│    Junction table linking students to guardians with role fl...
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), guardian_id(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; guardian_id → guardians(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ student_medical_record               → Prisma: StudentMedicalRecord
│    Medical master record per student — allergies, conditions...
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID)

│    Per-student document vault — birth cert, Aadhaar, photos,...

│    Periodic photo uploads for growth tracking + portfolio. D...
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), uploaded_by(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ student_passport                     → Prisma: StudentPassport
│    Optional passport/ECNR details for international transfer...
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE

14.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.

15. Domain: Academics
हा domain curriculum, lesson plans, observations, milestones, assessments, आणि report cards यांचा complete coverage आहे. NEP 2020 च्यa ECCE guidelines नुसार playgroup ते UKG पर्यंत age-appropriate learning outcomes defined आहेत. AI-assisted observation drafts + portfolio यांचा integration येथे आहे.
15.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Report card coverage
100% active students per period
Observation frequency
≥2 observations/student/week
Milestone tracking
≥95% students with milestone status
Lesson plan adherence
≥85% lessons delivered as planned
15.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 27 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:

15.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.

│    Curriculum offering — Playgroup, Nursery, LKG, UKG, Dayca...

│    Per-program curriculum definition with themes, subjects, ...

│
│  ◆ learning_outcome                     → Prisma: LearningOutcome
│    Reusable learning outcome catalog (cognitive, motor, soci...

│

│    Weekly lesson plan per classroom — themes, activities, le...
│    Key cols: classroom_id(UUID), curriculum_id(UUID), approved_by(UUID)
│    FKs: classroom_id → classrooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; curriculum_id → curriculums(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE

│    Master activity catalog — reusable across lesson plans.
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE

│  ◆ observation                          → Prisma: Observation
│    Teacher narrative note about a child's behavior, learning...

│    Item in a portfolio — artwork, worksheet, photo, certific...

15.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
15.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)

16. Domain: Daily Operations
हा domain preschool च्या दैनंदिन operations आहे — attendance, arrival/pickup tracking, meals, nap, toilet, mood, water intake, medicine administration, incident reports, आणि emergency logs. Today Dashboard चा data source दैनंदिन operations tables आहेत.
16.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Same-day attendance entry
≥99% by 10 AM
Daily report coverage
100% present students by 6 PM
Incident report SLA
100% within 1 hour
Pickup authorization compliance
100%
16.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 32 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:
Table
Prisma Model
Aggregate
Purpose
attendance
Attendance
Attendance
Per-student per-day attendance record with check-in/check-out timestamps.
attendance_bulk
AttendanceBulk
Attendance
Bulk attendance mark log — when teacher marks whole classroom at once.
attendance_correction
AttendanceCorrection
Attendance
Correction log for attendance after-the-fact changes.
arrival_log

16.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Daily Operations (32 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ attendance                           → Prisma: Attendance
│    Per-student per-day attendance record with check-in/check...
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), classroom_id(UUID), academic_session_id(UUID), pickup_guardian_id(UUI...
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; classroom_id → classrooms(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ attendance_bulk                      → Prisma: AttendanceBulk
│    Bulk attendance mark log — when teacher marks whole class...
│    Key cols: classroom_id(UUID), marked_by(UUID)
│    FKs: classroom_id → classrooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ attendance_correction                → Prisma: AttendanceCorrection
│    Correction log for attendance after-the-fact changes.
│    Key cols: attendance_id(UUID), corrected_by(UUID), approved_by(UUID)
│    FKs: attendance_id → attendances(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ arrival_log                          → Prisma: ArrivalLog
│    Real-time arrival log — when child enters premises.
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), dropped_by_guardian_id(UUID), gate_id(UUID), recorded_by(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ pickup_log                           → Prisma: PickupLog
│    Real-time pickup log — when child leaves premises.
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), picked_by_guardian_id(UUID), recorded_by(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ pickup_authorization                 → Prisma: PickupAuthorization
│    Per-student pickup authorization for non-guardian (relati...
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), granted_by_guardian_id(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; granted_by_guardian_id → guardians(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ late_pickup                          → Prisma: LatePickup
│    Late pickup tracking — drives late-pickup fee if applicable.
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), pickup_log_id(UUID), invoice_id(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; pickup_log_id → pickup_logs(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ meal_log                             → Prisma: MealLog
│    Per-student per-meal log — what they ate, how much.
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), recorded_by(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ meal_menu                            → Prisma: MealMenu
│    Daily/weekly meal menu per branch.
│    Key cols: branch_id(UUID)
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ nap_log                              → Prisma: NapLog
│    Per-student nap log — quality + duration.
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ... and 22 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└────────────────────────────────┘
16.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
16.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)
Most tables in this domain include the following common columns. They are omitted from individual table dictionaries for brevity but always present unless explicitly noted:

17. Domain: Inventory & Procurement
हा domain stock keeping units, purchase requests, POs, GRN, issue register, returns, damaged items, आणि stock audits यांचा complete workflow आहे. Reorder rules automated आहेत; low stock alerts threshold-based trigger होतात.
17.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Stock accuracy
≥98% post-audit
GRN-to-stock lag
≤4 hours
PO cycle time
Median ≤3 days
Stockout incidents
≤2 per quarter
17.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 26 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:
Table
Prisma Model
Aggregate
Purpose
inventory_category
InventoryCategory
Inventory
Inventory category dictionary — Toys, Montessori, Books, Art, etc.
inventory_item
InventoryItem
Inventory
Stock-keeping unit (SKU) master — name, category, unit, reorder level.
inventory_stock
InventoryStock
Inventory
Per-batch stock record — distinct from item summary. Tracks batch-level quantities.
stock_movement
StockMovement
Inventory
Append-only stock movement log — every in/out/adjustment.
purchase_request
PurchaseRequest
Inventory
Internal purchase request — staff raises; finance/head approves.
purchase_request_item
PurchaseRequestItem
Inventory
Line items in a purchase request.
purchase_order
PurchaseOrder
Inventory
Purchase order issued to vendor.
purchase_order_item
PurchaseOrderItem
Inventory
Line items in a purchase order.
grn
GRN
Inventory
Goods Receipt Note — acknowledges stock inward against a PO.
grn_item
GRNItem
Inventory
Line items in a GRN.
vendor
Vendor
Inventory
Supplier master — GST, contact, payment terms.
vendor_contact
VendorContact
Inventory
Multiple contacts per vendor.
stock_issue
StockIssue
Inventory
Stock issue to classroom/department/staff.
stock_issue_item
StockIssueItem
Inventory
Line items in a stock issue.
stock_return
StockReturn
Inventory
Stock return record — vendor return, internal return, or damaged return.
stock_return_item
StockReturnItem
Inventory
Line items in a stock return.
damaged_item
DamagedItem
Inventory
Damaged item record with disposal action.
damaged_action
DamagedAction
Inventory
Action log for damaged items (repair, dispose, vendor return).
stock_audit
StockAudit
Inventory
Stock audit (physical count) record per branch.
stock_audit_item
StockAuditItem
Inventory
Per-item audit count vs system count.
low_stock_alert
LowStockAlert
Inventory
Low stock alert record per item per trigger.
reorder_rule
ReorderRule
Inventory
Per-item auto-reorder rule.
kitchen_inventory
KitchenInventory
Inventory
Kitchen-specific stock tracking (food items, separate from general inventory).
kitchen_consumption
KitchenConsumption
Inventory
Daily kitchen consumption log per item.
supplier_invoice
SupplierInvoice
Inventory
Supplier/vendor invoice received against PO + GRN.
supplier_payment
SupplierPayment
Inventory
Payment made to supplier against invoice.
17.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Inventory & Procurement (26 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ inventory_category                   → Prisma: InventoryCategory
│    Inventory category dictionary — Toys, Montessori, Books, ...
│    Key cols: name(InventoryCategoryName)
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ inventory_item                       → Prisma: InventoryItem
│    Stock-keeping unit (SKU) master — name, category, unit, r...
│    Key cols: sku_code(varchar(16)), category_id(UUID), branch_id(UUID)
│    FKs: category_id → inventory_categories(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ inventory_stock                      → Prisma: InventoryStock
│    Per-batch stock record — distinct from item summary. Trac...
│    Key cols: item_id(UUID), grn_id(UUID)
│    FKs: item_id → inventory_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; grn_id → grns(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ stock_movement                       → Prisma: StockMovement
│    Append-only stock movement log — every in/out/adjustment.
│    Key cols: item_id(UUID), actor_id(UUID)
│    FKs: item_id → inventory_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ purchase_request                     → Prisma: PurchaseRequest
│    Internal purchase request — staff raises; finance/head ap...
│    Key cols: request_number(varchar(20)), branch_id(UUID), requested_by(UUID), approved_by(UUID), co...
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; requested_by → users(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ purchase_request_item                → Prisma: PurchaseRequestItem
│    Line items in a purchase request.
│    Key cols: purchase_request_id(UUID), item_id(UUID)
│    FKs: purchase_request_id → purchase_requests(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ purchase_order                       → Prisma: PurchaseOrder
│    Purchase order issued to vendor.
│    Key cols: po_number(varchar(20)), vendor_id(UUID), branch_id(UUID), purchase_request_id(UUID), is...
│    FKs: vendor_id → vendors(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ purchase_order_item                  → Prisma: PurchaseOrderItem
│    Line items in a purchase order.
│    Key cols: purchase_order_id(UUID), item_id(UUID)
│    FKs: purchase_order_id → purchase_orders(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ grn                                  → Prisma: GRN
│    Goods Receipt Note — acknowledges stock inward against a PO.
│    Key cols: grn_number(varchar(20)), purchase_order_id(UUID), vendor_id(UUID), branch_id(UUID), rec...
│    FKs: purchase_order_id → purchase_orders(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; vendor_id → vendors(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; +1 more
│
│  ◆ grn_item                             → Prisma: GRNItem
│    Line items in a GRN.
│    Key cols: grn_id(UUID), po_item_id(UUID), item_id(UUID)
│    FKs: grn_id → grns(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; item_id → inventory_items(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ... and 16 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└───────────────────────────────────────┘
17.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
17.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)
Most tables in this domain include the following common columns. They are omitted from individual table dictionaries for brevity but always present unless explicitly noted:
Column
Type
Null
Key
Description
id
UUID
NO
PK
Surrogate primary key (UUID v7)
school_id
UUID
NO
FK
Tenant anchor → schools(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT
branch_id
UUID
YES
FK
Branch scope → branches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE (nullable for school-wide tables)
created_at
timestamptz
NO
-
Row creation timestamp (UTC); set by trigger
updated_at
timestamptz
NO
-
Last modification timestamp (UTC); maintained by trigger
created_by
UUID
YES
FK
Actor → users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL (system actions leave NULL)
updated_by
UUID
YES
FK
Actor → users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL
deleted_at
timestamptz
YES
IDX
Soft-delete marker (NULL = active); partial index WHERE deleted_at IS NULL

18. Domain: Communication
हा domain parent messaging, announcements, broadcasts, events, RSVPs, आणि multi-channel delivery (SMS, WhatsApp, Email, Push) यांचा complete आहे. Delivery rate tracking + DLT compliance (India) + WhatsApp Business API integration येथे आहे.
18.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Delivery rate
≥98% across all channels
Read rate
≥75% for WhatsApp within 24h
Broadcast cost per month
Tracked per tenant
DLT compliance
100% templates registered
18.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 29 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:

18.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Communication (29 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ announcement                         → Prisma: Announcement
│    Announcement record — single source for all broadcast typ...
│    Key cols: branch_id(UUID), author_id(UUID)
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; author_id → users(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│

│    Per-recipient delivery record for an announcement.
│    Key cols: announcement_id(UUID), recipient_user_id(UUID)
│    FKs: announcement_id → announcements(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ broadcast                            → Prisma: Broadcast
│    Mass broadcast job — one broadcast to many recipients acr...
│    Key cols: template_id(UUID)
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ broadcast_log                        → Prisma: BroadcastLog
│    Per-recipient delivery log for a broadcast.
│    Key cols: broadcast_id(UUID), recipient_user_id(UUID)
│    FKs: broadcast_id → broadcasts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ sms_log                              → Prisma: SMSLog
│    Per-SMS delivery log.

│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE

│    Per-WhatsApp message delivery log.
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ email_log                            → Prisma: EmailLog
│    Per-email delivery log.
│    Key cols: branch_id(UUID), template_id(UUID)
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ push_log                             → Prisma: PushLog

18.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
18.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)
Most tables in this domain include the following common columns. They are omitted from individual table dictionaries for brevity but always present unless explicitly noted:

19. Domain: Finance
हा domain PreOne चा complete financial operations आहे — fee heads, fee plans, invoices, payments, receipts, GST, refunds, late fees, penalties, discounts, scholarships, expenses, income, आणि financial reports. BRC च्या Financial + Compliance rules या domain मध्ये enforce होतात.
19.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
DSO (Days Sales Outstanding)
≤15 days
Fee collection rate
≥95% within due date
GST compliance
100% filings on time
Reconciliation accuracy
100% bank ↔ system match
19.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 38 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:
Table
Prisma Model
Aggregate
Purpose
fee_head
FeeHead
Finance
Fee head master — tuition, transport, meal, activity, etc.
fee_plan
FeePlan
Finance
Fee plan — structured fee schedule per program.
fee_plan_item
FeePlanItem
Finance
Line items in a fee plan — fee heads with amounts.

FeeInstallment
Finance
Installment schedule per fee plan.

19.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Finance (38 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ fee_head                             → Prisma: FeeHead
│    Fee head master — tuition, transport, meal, activity, etc.
│    Key cols: code(varchar(16))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ fee_plan                             → Prisma: FeePlan
│    Fee plan — structured fee schedule per program.
│    Key cols: branch_id(UUID)
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ fee_plan_item                        → Prisma: FeePlanItem
│    Line items in a fee plan — fee heads with amounts.
│    Key cols: fee_plan_id(UUID), fee_head_id(UUID)
│    FKs: fee_plan_id → fee_plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; fee_head_id → fee_heads(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ fee_installment                      → Prisma: FeeInstallment
│    Installment schedule per fee plan.
│    Key cols: fee_plan_id(UUID)
│    FKs: fee_plan_id → fee_plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ fee_concession                       → Prisma: FeeConcession
│    Per-student concession — sibling, staff child, scholarshi...
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), fee_head_id(UUID), approved_by(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; fee_head_id → fee_heads(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ discount                             → Prisma: Discount
│    Discount master — early-bird, sibling, staff, etc.
│    Key cols: code(varchar(16)), fee_head_id(UUID)
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ discount_approval                    → Prisma: DiscountApproval
│    Approval record for discounts applied to invoices.
│    Key cols: invoice_id(UUID), discount_id(UUID), requested_by(UUID), approved_by(UUID)
│    FKs: invoice_id → invoices(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ scholarship                          → Prisma: Scholarship
│    Scholarship program master.
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ scholarship_award                    → Prisma: ScholarshipAward
│    Per-student scholarship award record.
│    Key cols: scholarship_id(UUID), student_id(UUID), awarded_by(UUID), academic_session_id(UUID)
│    FKs: scholarship_id → scholarships(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; academic_session_id → academic_sessions(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; +1 more
│
│  ◆ penalty_rule                         → Prisma: PenaltyRule
│    Late fee penalty rule — fixed/day, fixed/instance, or per...
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ... and 28 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└───────────────────────┘
19.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
19.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)
Most tables in this domain include the following common columns. They are omitted from individual table dictionaries for brevity but always present unless explicitly noted:

20. Domain: Human Resources
हा domain staff master, payroll, leave, attendance, recruitment, onboarding, offboarding, आणि performance reviews यांचा complete आहे. Payroll cycle monthly आहे; payslips auto-generated आहेत. POSH compliance + staff background checks येथे enforce होतात.
20.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Payroll cycle time
≤3 days from month-end
Leave approval TAT
Median ≤24 hours
Background check coverage
100% staff verified
Attrition rate
≤15% annual
20.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 31 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:

20.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Human Resources (31 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ department                           → Prisma: Department
│    Department master — Teaching, Admin, Transport, etc.
│    Key cols: name(varchar(64))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ designation                          → Prisma: Designation
│    Designation master — Principal, Teacher, Helper, etc.
│    Key cols: name(varchar(64)), department_id(UUID)
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ staff                                → Prisma: Staff
│    Staff master record. Linked 1:1 to user account for login.
│    Key cols: user_id(UUID), employee_code(varchar(16)), department_id(UUID), designation_id(UUID), b...
│    FKs: user_id → users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; department_id → departments(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; +2 more
│
│  ◆ staff_profile                        → Prisma: StaffProfile
│    Extended staff profile — personal details, address, emerg...
│    Key cols: staff_id(UUID)
│    FKs: staff_id → staff(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ staff_document                       → Prisma: StaffDocument
│    Staff document vault — ID proofs, qualification certs, ex...
│    Key cols: staff_id(UUID), verified_by(UUID)
│    FKs: staff_id → staff(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ staff_qualification                  → Prisma: StaffQualification
│    Per-staff qualification records.
│    Key cols: staff_id(UUID)
│    FKs: staff_id → staff(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ staff_experience                     → Prisma: StaffExperience
│    Prior experience records per staff.
│    Key cols: staff_id(UUID)
│    FKs: staff_id → staff(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ staff_bank_detail                    → Prisma: StaffBankDetail
│    Bank account for payroll (encrypted).
│    Key cols: staff_id(UUID)
│    FKs: staff_id → staff(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ employment_type                      → Prisma: EmploymentType
│    Employment type master — full-time, part-time, contract.
│    Key cols: name(varchar(32))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ payroll                              → Prisma: Payroll
│    Monthly payroll batch per branch.
│    Key cols: payroll_number(varchar(20)), branch_id(UUID), processed_by(UUID)
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ... and 21 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└───────────────────────────────┘
20.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
20.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)
Most tables in this domain include the following common columns. They are omitted from individual table dictionaries for brevity but always present unless explicitly noted:

20.4.2 department

21. Domain: Administration
हा domain physical infrastructure + general administration आहे — rooms, activity rooms, assets, maintenance, visitor management, compliance tracking, drivers. Compliance DPDP/POSH/NBC/FSSAI/RTE चे records येथे maintain होतात.
21.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Compliance currency
100% licenses valid
Asset tracking accuracy
≥98%
Maintenance response time
Median ≤24 hours
Visitor log completeness
100%
21.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 18 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:

Prisma Model

21.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Administration (18 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ room                                 → Prisma: Room
│    Physical room master — classrooms, offices, activity rooms.
│    Key cols: code(varchar(16)), branch_id(UUID)
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ activity_room                        → Prisma: ActivityRoom
│    Activity-specific room — gym, music room, art room.
│    Key cols: room_id(UUID)
│    FKs: room_id → rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ room_booking                         → Prisma: RoomBooking
│    Room booking for events/activities.
│    Key cols: room_id(UUID), booked_by(UUID)
│    FKs: room_id → rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ asset                                → Prisma: Asset
│    Asset master — furniture, equipment, IT devices.
│    Key cols: asset_code(varchar(20)), category_id(UUID), branch_id(UUID), room_id(UUID)
│    FKs: category_id → asset_categories(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; room_id → rooms(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; +1 more
│
│  ◆ asset_category                       → Prisma: AssetCategory
│    Asset category master.
│    Key cols: name(varchar(64))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ asset_movement                       → Prisma: AssetMovement
│    Asset movement log — transfer between rooms/branches.
│    Key cols: asset_id(UUID), from_room_id(UUID), to_room_id(UUID), from_branch_id(UUID), to_branch_i...
│    FKs: asset_id → assets(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ asset_maintenance                    → Prisma: AssetMaintenance
│    Asset maintenance log.
│    Key cols: asset_id(UUID), vendor_id(UUID)
│    FKs: asset_id → assets(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ maintenance_request                  → Prisma: MaintenanceRequest
│    Maintenance request for facilities (plumbing, electrical,...
│    Key cols: request_number(varchar(20)), branch_id(UUID), room_id(UUID), asset_id(UUID), requested_...
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; room_id → rooms(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; asset_id → assets(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; +1 more
│
│  ◆ maintenance_log                      → Prisma: MaintenanceLog
│    Per-request maintenance action log.
│    Key cols: maintenance_request_id(UUID), actor_id(UUID)
│    FKs: maintenance_request_id → maintenance_requests(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ visitor                              → Prisma: Visitor
│    Visitor master record (returning visitors).
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ... and 8 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└──────────────────────────────┘
21.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
21.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)
Most tables in this domain include the following common columns. They are omitted from individual table dictionaries for brevity but always present unless explicitly noted:

22. Domain: Transport
हा domain transport routes, stops, student assignments, trips, GPS tracking, आणि transport fee management आहे. Driver + Vehicle master Administration domain मध्ये आहेत; route operations येथे.
22.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
On-time drop rate
≥95%
Route utilization
≥70% capacity
Transport attendance coverage
100% trips
GPS ping interval
≤30 seconds
22.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 11 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:
Table
Prisma Model
Aggregate
Purpose
transport_route
TransportRoute
Transport
Transport route master — pickup/drop sequence with stops.
route_stop
RouteStop
Transport
Stop in a transport route — sequence + times.
route_student
RouteStudent
Transport
Student ↔ route + stop assignment.
vehicle_document
VehicleDocument
Transport
Vehicle document vault — RC, insurance, PUC, fitness.
driver_document
DriverDocument
Transport
Driver document vault — license, police verification, medical.
trip
Trip
Transport
Per-day trip record — morning pickup or evening drop.
trip_log
TripLog
Transport
GPS + event log per trip.
transport_attendance
TransportAttendance
Transport
Per-trip per-student pickup/drop attendance.
transport_fee
TransportFee
Transport
Per-student transport fee configuration per route.
pickup_authorization
PickupAuthorizationTransport
Transport
Pickup authorization specific to transport — who can receive child at stop.
transport_route_alternate
TransportRouteAlternate
Transport
Alternate route when primary route is unavailable (vehicle breakdown, driver absent).
22.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Transport (11 tables) ─┐
│
│  ◆ transport_route                      → Prisma: TransportRoute
│    Transport route master — pickup/drop sequence with stops.
│    Key cols: route_code(varchar(16)), branch_id(UUID), vehicle_id(UUID), driver_id(UUID), attendant_...
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; vehicle_id → vehicles(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; driver_id → drivers(id) ON DELETE SET NULL; +1 more
│
│  ◆ route_stop                           → Prisma: RouteStop
│    Stop in a transport route — sequence + times.
│    Key cols: route_id(UUID)
│    FKs: route_id → transport_routes(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ route_student                        → Prisma: RouteStudent
│    Student ↔ route + stop assignment.
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), route_id(UUID), stop_id(UUID), academic_session_id(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; route_id → transport_routes(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; stop_id → route_stops(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; +2 more
│
│  ◆ vehicle_document                     → Prisma: VehicleDocument
│    Vehicle document vault — RC, insurance, PUC, fitness.
│    Key cols: vehicle_id(UUID)
│    FKs: vehicle_id → vehicles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ driver_document                      → Prisma: DriverDocument
│    Driver document vault — license, police verification, med...
│    Key cols: driver_id(UUID)
│    FKs: driver_id → drivers(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ trip                                 → Prisma: Trip
│    Per-day trip record — morning pickup or evening drop.
│    Key cols: route_id(UUID), vehicle_id(UUID), driver_id(UUID)
│    FKs: route_id → transport_routes(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; vehicle_id → vehicles(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; driver_id → drivers(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; +1 more
│
│  ◆ trip_log                             → Prisma: TripLog
│    GPS + event log per trip.
│    Key cols: trip_id(UUID), stop_id(UUID), student_id(UUID)
│    FKs: trip_id → trips(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ transport_attendance                 → Prisma: TransportAttendance
│    Per-trip per-student pickup/drop attendance.
│    Key cols: trip_id(UUID), student_id(UUID), stop_id(UUID)
│    FKs: trip_id → trips(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ transport_fee                        → Prisma: TransportFee
│    Per-student transport fee configuration per route.
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), route_id(UUID), academic_session_id(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; route_id → transport_routes(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; academic_session_id → academic_sessions(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; +1 more
│
│  ◆ pickup_authorization                 → Prisma: PickupAuthorizationTransport
│    Pickup authorization specific to transport — who can rece...
│    Key cols: student_id(UUID), route_id(UUID), granted_by_guardian_id(UUID)
│    FKs: student_id → students(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; route_id → transport_routes(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; granted_by_guardian_id → guardians(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT; +1 more
│
│  ... and 1 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└─────────────────────────┘
22.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
22.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)

23. Domain: Settings
हा domain school/branch-level configuration आहे — academic sessions, calendar, working days, holidays, report configurations, audit log (cross-cutting), integration configs, notification rules, scheduled jobs, system settings, feature flags, locale resources.
23.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Config propagation
<60 sec to all instances
Calendar accuracy
100% working days per session
Scheduled job success rate
≥99%
Audit log retention compliance
100% per DPDP §17
23.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 12 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:

Prisma Model
Aggregate

23.3 ERD Diagram
खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.
┌─ Settings (12 tables) ─┐
