│    Key cols: branch_id(UUID)
│    FKs: branch_id → branches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ working_day                          → Prisma: WorkingDay
│    Working day configuration — which weekdays are working.
│    Key cols: branch_id(UUID), academic_session_id(UUID)

│  ◆ report_config                        → Prisma: ReportConfig
│    Report configuration — schedule, format, recipients.

│  ◆ integration_config                   → Prisma: IntegrationConfig
│    Branch-level integration configuration (distinct from sch...

│  ◆ schedule_job                         → Prisma: ScheduleJob
│    Scheduled job — recurring background task.

│

│    School-level system settings — key/value config.

23.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.
23.4.1 Common Audit Columns (auto-injected)

24. Domain: Cross-Cutting / Shared
हा domain cross-cutting infrastructure tables आहेत — file uploads, queues (SMS/WhatsApp/Email/Job), webhook outbox, event store, snapshots, locks, sequence counters, health checks. या tables सर्व domains cross-cut करतात.
24.1 Domain KPIs
या domain चे operational health measure करणारे KPIs खालीलप्रमाणे आहेत:
KPI
Target / Definition
Queue throughput
≥1000 messages/min
Webhook delivery success
≥99%
File upload success
≥99.5%
Lock contention rate
≤1%
24.2 Table Inventory
या domain मध्ये 12 tables आहेत. खालील summary table प्रत्येक table चे name, Prisma model, aggregate, आणि purpose capture करते:

Prisma Model

खालील ASCII diagram domain च्या primary tables आणि त्यांच्या एकमेकांशी FK relationships दर्शवतो. हे diagram simplified आहे — complete FK list प्रत्येक table च्या data dictionary मध्ये document आहे.

│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ sms_queue                            → Prisma: SMSQueue
│    Outbound SMS queue.
│    Key cols: template_id(UUID)
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ whatsapp_queue                       → Prisma: WhatsAppQueue
│    Outbound WhatsApp queue.
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ job_queue                            → Prisma: JobQueue
│    General-purpose background job queue.
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ webhook_outbox                       → Prisma: WebhookOutbox
│    Outbound webhook outbox — pattern for reliable delivery.
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ event_store                          → Prisma: EventStore
│    Append-only event store for event sourcing pattern.
│    Key cols: actor_id(UUID)
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ snapshot                             → Prisma: Snapshot
│    Aggregate snapshot — for event sourcing optimization.
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ◆ lock                                 → Prisma: Lock
│    Distributed lock — for concurrent job execution prevention.
│    Key cols: lock_key(varchar(64))
│    FKs: school_id → schools(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
│
│  ... and 2 more tables (see Data Dictionary below)
│
└──────────────────────────────────────┘
24.4 Data Dictionary
खालील subsections मध्ये domain च्या प्रत्येक table ची column-level data dictionary आहे. प्रत्येक table साठी: (a) purpose, (b) column list [name, type, nullable, key, description], (c) indexes, (d) foreign keys, (e) Prisma model name. Common columns (id, school_id, branch_id, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at) सर्वत्र inject होतात आणि standard audit columns म्हणून documented आहेत.

26. Aggregate → Table Mapping (DDD Trail)
हा chapter DDD v1.0 च्या Section 24 चा expansion आहे. प्रत्येक DDD aggregate ची physical table implementation येथे document आहे. हे mapping AI code generators साठी critical आहे — given an aggregate, AI tool ला exact tables आणि their relationships शी map करता येते.

27. Prisma Schema Mapping
Prisma हा PreOne चा ORM आहे — TypeScript-first schema definition, type-safe queries, आणि automatic migrations. या chapter मध्ये database tables → Prisma models चे mapping + standard annotations document आहेत.
27.1 Naming Conventions
•  Table name (snake_case) → Prisma model (PascalCase): students → Student, audit_log → AuditLog.
•  Column name (snake_case) → Prisma field (camelCase): school_id → schoolId, created_at → createdAt.
•  @@map annotation on model to specify table name.
•  @map annotation on field to specify column name.
•  @@unique for composite unique constraints.
•  @@index for composite indexes.
•  Enum types defined at top of schema file; values UPPER_SNAKE_CASE.
27.2 Sample Prisma Model
Student table चे Prisma model definition खालीलप्रमाणे आहे — याच pattern सर्व tables साठी follow केला जातो:
model Student {
  id                  String        @id @default(uuid()) @db.Uuid
  schoolId            String        @map("school_id") @db.Uuid
  branchId            String?       @map("branch_id") @db.Uuid
  studentCode         String        @unique @map("student_code")
  admissionId         String?       @map("admission_id") @db.Uuid
  firstName           String        @map("first_name")
  lastName            String        @map("last_name")
  dob                 DateTime      @db.Date
  gender              Gender
  bloodGroup          BloodGroup?   @map("blood_group")
  status              StudentStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  currentBranchId     String?       @map("current_branch_id") @db.Uuid
  currentClassroomId  String?       @map("current_classroom_id") @db.Uuid
  currentProgram      ProgramType?  @map("current_program")
  admissionDate       DateTime      @db.Date @map("admission_date")
  exitDate            DateTime?     @db.Date @map("exit_date")
  exitType            ExitType?     @map("exit_type")
  createdAt           DateTime      @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt           DateTime      @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  deletedAt           DateTime?     @map("deleted_at")
 
  school              School        @relation(fields: [schoolId], references: [id], onDelete: Restrict)
  branch              Branch?       @relation(fields: [branchId], references: [id], onDelete: SetNull)
  admission           Admission?    @relation(fields: [admissionId], references: [id], onDelete: SetNull)
  currentBranch       Branch?       @relation("StudentCurrentBranch", fields: [currentBranchId], references: [id], onDelete: SetNull)
  currentClassroom    Classroom?    @relation(fields: [currentClassroomId], references: [id], onDelete: SetNull)
 
  attendances         Attendance[]
  observations        Observation[]
  invoices            Invoice[]
  classroomAssignments ClassroomAssignment[]
 
  @@index([branchId, status])
  @@index([currentBranchId, status])
  @@map("students")
}

28. Migration Strategy (v2 → v3)
v2 → v3 migration हा large-scale schema evolution आहे — 142 tables पासून 307 tables पर्यंत, plus multi-tenancy layer hardening, partitioning introduction, आणि DPDP compliance fields. या chapter मध्ये phased migration plan document आहे.
28.1 Migration Waves
Migration 12 waves मध्ये execute होतो — दर wave 1-2 weeks मध्ये complete होतो. दर wave ची deploy + verify + rollback plan documented आहे.
Wave
Scope
Duration
Risk
W1
Add school_id NOT NULL to all tenant-scoped tables; backfill from existing branch.school_id
2 weeks
High — large backfill
W2
Introduce RLS policies + app.school_id session variable
1 week
Medium — connection pool changes
W3
Add deleted_at column to all soft-delete tables; partial indexes
1 week
Low
W4
Normalize enum types — convert varchar status columns to native PG enums where stable
2 weeks
Medium — data conversion
W5
Add jsonb config columns to replace scattered text columns
1 week
Low
W6
Create audit_log partitioning + BRIN indexes
1 week
Medium — partition setup
W7
Build all missing indexes CONCURRENTLY (zero-downtime)
3 weeks
Medium — long-running
W8
Deploy read replica + application read-routing layer
2 weeks
High — connection routing
W9
Add DPDP compliance fields (consent, retention_until, data_minimized)
1 week
Low
W10
Migrate PII columns to pgcrypto encryption
3 weeks
High — data migration
W11
Switch application to v3 schema (dual-write during transition)
2 weeks
High — application changes
W12
Decommission v2 schema + final cutover
1 week
Medium — rollback risk
28.2 Rollback Plan
दर wave साठी rollback plan documented आहे — schema snapshot before migration, dual-write window where possible, feature flag to revert to v2 logic. Total rollback window 30 days from W11 cutover. Post-W12, rollback requires data loss (v3-only columns).
28.3 Verification
दर wave post-deploy verification: (a) row count parity, (b) query performance regression test, (c) application smoke test suite, (d) audit log completeness check, (e) RLS isolation test (cross-tenant query must return 0 rows).
29. Backup, Restore & DR
Backup + Restore + Disaster Recovery strategy हा PreOne चा business continuity backbone आहे. या chapter मध्ये operational procedures + RPO/RTO targets + drill cadence document आहेत.
29.1 Backup Strategy
Backup Type
Frequency
Retention
Storage
Purpose
WAL archive
Continuous
30 days
S3 (cross-region)
PITR — point-in-time recovery
Logical backup (pg_dump, per tenant)
Daily 02:00 UTC
90 days
S3 (encrypted)
Single-tenant granular restore
Full cluster snapshot
Weekly Sun 01:00 UTC
12 weeks
EBS snapshot + S3
Full cluster restore
Monthly archive backup
1st of month
7 years
S3 Glacier Deep Archive
Regulatory retention
29.2 Restore Procedures
•  Single-row restore: PITR WAL replay to staging → extract row → INSERT into production (manual review).
•  Single-tenant restore: pg_dump from daily backup → restore to staging → extract tenant rows → INSERT/UPDATE into production.
•  Schema migration rollback: Snapshot restore to staging → reverse migration → verify → promote.
•  Primary failure: Promote sync replica → update DNS → restart app servers.
•  Region failure: Promote cross-region DR replica → update Route53 → failback after primary region recovery.

30.3 Partitioning Strategy
Time-series tables (audit_log, sms_log, whatsapp_log, email_log, trip_log, attendances, daily_reports, meal_logs, event_store, broadcast_logs, announcement_recipients, medical_logs) हे monthly किंवा yearly partitioned आहेत. PostgreSQL 16 native partitioning (declarative) use केले जाते. Old partitions DETACH + archive to cold storage (S3 Glacier) after 12 months; DETACH is non-blocking.
30.4 Archival Policy
Data Type
Hot Retention
Cold Retention
Action
Audit logs
12 months (PostgreSQL)
7 years (S3 Glacier)
Detach + archive monthly
SMS/WhatsApp/Email logs
6 months (PostgreSQL)
2 years (S3 Glacier)
Detach + archive quarterly
Attendance logs
3 years (PostgreSQL)
7 years (S3 Glacier)
Detach + archive yearly
Daily reports
2 years (PostgreSQL)
5 years (S3 Glacier)
Detach + archive yearly

7 years (PostgreSQL)
Anonymized forever
Scrub PII + retain aggregate
Financial records
7 years (PostgreSQL)
10 years (S3 Glacier)
Regulatory (GST)
Marketing data (lost leads)
2 years (PostgreSQL)
None
Hard delete after 2 years per DPDP §17
31. Glossary & Document Control
31.1 Glossary
या Document मध्ये वापरलेल्या database terms चा authoritative reference खालील आहे:
Term
Definition
ACID
Atomicity, Consistency, Isolation, Durability — transaction guarantees
BRIN
Block Range Index — compact index for naturally-ordered data (time-series)
CASCADE
FK ON DELETE behavior — child rows auto-deleted with parent
CDC
Change Data Capture — pattern for streaming DB changes to downstream systems
CHECK Constraint
Domain constraint enforcing column value conditions
citext
Case-insensitive text type — auto-lowercases for comparison
DLT
Distributed Ledger Technology — India TRAI mandate for SMS sender registration
DPDP
Digital Personal Data Protection Act 2023 (India)
DSAR
Data Subject Access Request — DPDP §11 right to access
ETL
Extract, Transform, Load — data warehouse pipeline
EXCLUDE Constraint
Prevents overlapping ranges (e.g., room bookings)
FK
Foreign Key — referential integrity constraint
GIN
Generalized Inverted Index — for jsonb, array containment queries
GiST
Generalized Search Tree — for geometric, range, full-text
jsonb
Binary JSON — queryable, indexable JSON storage
MRR
Monthly Recurring Revenue — SaaS metric
MVCC
Multi-Version Concurrency Control — PostgreSQL's isolation mechanism
NOC
No Objection Certificate
Partitioning
Splitting large tables into smaller physical pieces
pgcrypto
PostgreSQL extension for encryption functions
PITR
Point-In-Time Recovery — restore to specific timestamp via WAL replay
PK
Primary Key — row uniqueness
PO
Purchase Order
RPO
Recovery Point Objective — max acceptable data loss
RLS
Row-Level Security — tenant isolation at DB layer
RTO
Recovery Time Objective — max acceptable downtime
SET NULL
FK ON DELETE behavior — child FK set to NULL on parent delete
SaaS
Software as a Service
TDE
Transparent Data Encryption — disk-level encryption
TDS
Tax Deducted at Source (India)
TTL
Time To Live — auto-expiration
UQ
Unique constraint
UUID v7
Time-sortable UUID — preferred for distributed PK generation
WAL
Write-Ahead Log — PostgreSQL's durability mechanism
